# Test source

```ts
   1 | import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
   2 | import { AmazonPage } from '../src/pages/amazon-page';
   3 | import { AmazonNavElement } from '../src/elements/amazon-nav-horizontal-links';
   4 | import { AmazonCardSection } from '../src/elements/amazon-4-cards-section';
   5 | import { AmazonHamburgerMenu } from '../src/elements/amazon-hamburger-menu.element';
   6 | test.use({ storageState: './browser-context.json' });
   7 |
   8 | test.describe('Amazon tests', () => {
   9 |     let amazonPage: AmazonPage;
  10 |
  11 |     test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
  12 |         amazonPage = new AmazonPage(page);
  13 |     });
  14 |     test('should search and check results', async () => {
  15 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  16 |         await amazonPage.search('chair');
  17 |
  18 |         const hasKeyword = await amazonPage.verifySearchResults('Chair');
> 19 |         expect(hasKeyword).toBeTruthy();
     |                            ^ Error: expect(received).toBeTruthy()
  20 |     });
  21 |
  22 |     test('should check product page options', async () => {
  23 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  24 |         await amazonPage.search('chair');
  25 |         await amazonPage.selectRandomProduct();
  26 |
  27 |         const hasOptions = await amazonPage.verifyProductOptions();
  28 |         expect(hasOptions).toBeTruthy();
  29 |     });
  30 |
  31 |     test('should select a sort option from the dropdown', async () => {
  32 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  33 |         await amazonPage.search('chair');
  34 |         await amazonPage.selectSortOption();
  35 |     });
  36 |     test('should click on selected specific nav link', async ({ page }) => {
  37 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  38 |         const nav = new AmazonNavElement(page.locator('#nav-xshop'));
  39 |         const names = await nav.getLinkNames();
  40 |         console.log('Tab names:', names);
  41 |
  42 |         await nav.selectLink('Prime Video');
  43 |
  44 |     });
  45 |
  46 |     test('should click on random nav link', async ({ page }) => {
  47 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  48 |
  49 |         const nav = new AmazonNavElement(page.locator('#nav-xshop'));
  50 |
  51 |         const clickedTab = await nav.selectRandomLink();
  52 |         console.log('Clicked random tab:', clickedTab);
  53 |     });
  54 |
  55 |     test('should click random valid card section and verify text', async ({ page }) => {
  56 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  57 |         const cardsBlock = new AmazonCardSection(page);
  58 |         const validCard = await cardsBlock.selectRandomValidCard();
  59 |         const sectionText = await cardsBlock.clickRandomSectionInCard(validCard);
  60 |         await cardsBlock.verifyTextOnPage(sectionText);
  61 |     });
  62 |
  63 |     test('should open hamburger menu and verify greeting', async ({ page }) => {
  64 |         await amazonPage.goTo();
  65 |         const hamburgerMenu = new AmazonHamburgerMenu(page);
  66 |         await hamburgerMenu.openMenu();
  67 |         await hamburgerMenu.verifyCustomerGreeting();
  68 |     });
  69 |
  70 | });
```
